  id = demob.8
  title = demob.1.t

    is_ai = yes
    has_army_size = {
      size > 50

  id = demob.15
  title = demob.1.t
  desc = demob.1.d
  picture = GFX_demobilization_event

  fire_only_once = yes

  trigger = {
    is_ai = yes
    has_army_size = {
      size > 50

    has_war = no

  id = demob.18
  title = demob.1.t
  desc = demob.1.d

  fire_only_once = yes

  trigger = {
    is_ai = yes
    has_army_size = {
      size > 50
